## [16:23:54] Orchestrator: PROMPT (第 1 轮)
### 📋 完整Prompt内容
```
下面给你的内容是搜索到的内容经评估后的结果，你要查看这些结果然后选择适当的内容进行扩展或者想到新的方面进行进一步的研究。证据节点ID: 5705d0e4-8952-48fe-aa24-6e4b3a4e88c5, 选择了strategy_semantic_search工具, 工具参数为{'query_intent': 'experiment studying air pollution'}。
                        本次是第1次检索到, 评估人员已评估，评估分数为{'relevance': 8, 'credibility': 9},认为其内容应该[GROW]。
                        具体而言评估人员总结条目内容为该研究通过隧道内的移动实验测量了真实交通条件下的车辆排放因子，并发现在隧道内针对 $\mathrm{CO}_{2}$, $\mathrm{SO}_{2}$, 和 $\mathrm{NO}_{\mathrm{X}}$ 排放可以设定一个不受环境空气混合效应影响的起点。这些数据有助于理解隧道内空气污染物的混合和累积区域。,理由是该证据提供了详细的排放因子数据和验证结果，为政策制定和空气质量管理提供了实用价值。,他抽取处理一些关键词推荐给你['Vehicle emission factors', 'Mobile laboratory', 'Tunnel environment']。
                        这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Mobile measurement of vehicle emission factors in _1', 'text': 'Tunnels are the preferred experimental environments for estimating vehicle emission factors (EFs) under real-world driving conditions. In this study, online measurements of traffic-related air pollutants (including  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{O}_{3}$ , particulate matter [PM], and volatile organic compounds [VOCs]) were conducted using a mobile laboratory in the Sujungsan Tunnel in Busan, Korea. Mobile measurements generated concentration profiles of the target exhaust emissions inside the tunnel. These data were used to produce a zonation of the tunnel, i.e., mixing and accumulation zones. There were differences between the  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ , and  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$  profiles, and a starting point that was free from ambient air mixing effects could be set at  $600\\mathrm{m}$  from the tunnel entrance. The EFs of vehicle exhaust emissions were calculated using pollutant concentration gradients. The average EFs for  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ , NO,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{10}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$ , and  $\\sum \\mathrm{VOCs}$  were 149,000, 380, 55, 29.2, 9.64, 4.33, and  $16.7\\mathrm{mgkm}^{-1}\\cdot \\mathrm{veh}^{-1}$ , respectively. Among the VOC groups, alkanes contributed more than  $70\\%$  of the VOC EF. Mobile measurement-derived EFs were validated using the conventional EFs from stationary measurements. The EF results from the mobile measurements matched those from the stationary measurements, while the absolute concentration differences between them implied complex aerodynamic movements of the target pollutants inside the tunnel. This study demonstrated the usefulness and advantages of applying mobile measurements in a tunnel environment and indicated the potential of the approach for observation-based policymaking.\n\n# 1.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Mobile measurement of vehicle emission factors in ', 'text': 'Tunnels are the preferred experimental environments for estimating vehicle emission factors (EFs) under real-world driving conditions. In this study, online measurements of traffic-related air pollutants (including  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{O}_{3}$ , particulate matter [PM], and volatile organic compounds [VOCs]) were conducted using a mobile laboratory in the Sujungsan Tunnel in Busan, Korea. Mobile measurements generated concentration profiles of the target exhaust emissions inside the tunnel. These data were used to produce a zonation of the tunnel, i.e., mixing and accumulation zones. There were differences between the  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ , and  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$  profiles, and a starting point that was free from ambient air mixing effects could be set at  $600\\mathrm{m}$  from the tunnel entrance. The EFs of vehicle exhaust emissions were calculated using pollutant concentration gradients. The average EFs for  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ , NO,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{10}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$ , and  $\\sum \\mathrm{VOCs}$  were 149,000, 380, 55, 29.2, 9.64, 4.33, and  $16.7\\mathrm{mgkm}^{-1}\\cdot \\mathrm{veh}^{-1}$ , respectively. Among the VOC groups, alkanes contributed more than  $70\\%$  of the VOC EF. Mobile measurement-derived EFs were validated using the conventional EFs from stationary measurements. The EF results from the mobile measurements matched those from the stationary measurements, while the absolute concentration differences between them implied complex aerodynamic movements of the target pollutants inside the tunnel. This study demonstrated the usefulness and advantages of applying mobile measurements in a tunnel environment and indicated the potential of the approach for observation-based policymaking.\n\n# 1.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Mobile measurement of vehicle emission factors in ', 'text': 'Tunnels are the preferred experimental environments for estimating vehicle emission factors (EFs) under real-world driving conditions. In this study, online measurements of traffic-related air pollutants (including  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{O}_{3}$ , particulate matter [PM], and volatile organic compounds [VOCs]) were conducted using a mobile laboratory in the Sujungsan Tunnel in Busan, Korea. Mobile measurements generated concentration profiles of the target exhaust emissions inside the tunnel. These data were used to produce a zonation of the tunnel, i.e., mixing and accumulation zones. There were differences between the  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ , and  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$  profiles, and a starting point that was free from ambient air mixing effects could be set at  $600\\mathrm{m}$  from the tunnel entrance. The EFs of vehicle exhaust emissions were calculated using pollutant concentration gradients. The average EFs for  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ , NO,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{10}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$ , and  $\\sum \\mathrm{VOCs}$  were 149,000, 380, 55, 29.2, 9.64, 4.33, and  $16.7\\mathrm{mgkm}^{-1}\\cdot \\mathrm{veh}^{-1}$ , respectively. Among the VOC groups, alkanes contributed more than  $70\\%$  of the VOC EF. Mobile measurement-derived EFs were validated using the conventional EFs from stationary measurements. The EF results from the mobile measurements matched those from the stationary measurements, while the absolute concentration differences between them implied complex aerodynamic movements of the target pollutants inside the tunnel. This study demonstrated the usefulness and advantages of applying mobile measurements in a tunnel environment and indicated the potential of the approach for observation-based policymaking.\n\n# 1. The safety issues and logistical difficulties in setting up analytical instrumentation inside a tunnel were overcome using a mobile laboratory. The heavy traffic in the urban tunnel did not enable sufficient room for the instrumentation and researchers to operate; thus, safety issues affected the operation of the research. Multipoint data generated by online instruments in a mobile laboratory can also help to overcome the various uncertainties associated with stationary measurements. This study identified a zonation inside the tunnel, i.e., mixing and accumulation zones, and recommended that the mixing zone be avoided to ensure accurate EF measurements. The concept of a concentration gradient was applied for EF calculations. The EF results from the mobile measurements were well matched with those from stationary measurements, while the absolute concentration differences between them suggested that further studies are required to assess the complex aerodynamic movements of the pollutants inside the tunnel. The proposed mobile measurement approach has potential for use in future tunnel studies. Because vehicle exhaust is recognized as one of the main sources of primary and secondary PM in large cities worldwide, there is an increasing need for more frequent and region-specific measurements of EFs in real environments for timely policymaking. Tunnel studies with mobile measurements can provide the required information.\n\n# Author contributions statement', 'summary': 'This study determined the usefulness and advantages of making mobile measurements of exhaust pollutants in a tunnel study.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Mobile measurement of vehicle emission factors in _1', 'text': 'Tunnels are the preferred experimental environments for estimating vehicle emission factors (EFs) under real-world driving conditions. In this study, online measurements of traffic-related air pollutants (including  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{O}_{3}$ , particulate matter [PM], and volatile organic compounds [VOCs]) were conducted using a mobile laboratory in the Sujungsan Tunnel in Busan, Korea. Mobile measurements generated concentration profiles of the target exhaust emissions inside the tunnel. These data were used to produce a zonation of the tunnel, i.e., mixing and accumulation zones. There were differences between the  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ , and  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$  profiles, and a starting point that was free from ambient air mixing effects could be set at  $600\\mathrm{m}$  from the tunnel entrance. The EFs of vehicle exhaust emissions were calculated using pollutant concentration gradients. The average EFs for  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ , NO,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{10}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$ , and  $\\sum \\mathrm{VOCs}$  were 149,000, 380, 55, 29.2, 9.64, 4.33, and  $16.7\\mathrm{mgkm}^{-1}\\cdot \\mathrm{veh}^{-1}$ , respectively. Among the VOC groups, alkanes contributed more than  $70\\%$  of the VOC EF. Mobile measurement-derived EFs were validated using the conventional EFs from stationary measurements. The EF results from the mobile measurements matched those from the stationary measurements, while the absolute concentration differences between them implied complex aerodynamic movements of the target pollutants inside the tunnel. This study demonstrated the usefulness and advantages of applying mobile measurements in a tunnel environment and indicated the potential of the approach for observation-based policymaking.\n\n# 1.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Mobile measurement of vehicle emission factors in _1', 'text': 'This study determined the usefulness and advantages of making mobile measurements of exhaust pollutants in a tunnel study. The safety issues and logistical difficulties in setting up analytical instrumentation inside a tunnel were overcome using a mobile laboratory. The heavy traffic in the urban tunnel did not enable sufficient room for the instrumentation and researchers to operate; thus, safety issues affected the operation of the research. Multipoint data generated by online instruments in a mobile laboratory can also help to overcome the various uncertainties associated with stationary measurements. This study identified a zonation inside the tunnel, i.e., mixing and accumulation zones, and recommended that the mixing zone be avoided to ensure accurate EF measurements. The concept of a concentration gradient was applied for EF calculations. The EF results from the mobile measurements were well matched with those from stationary measurements, while the absolute concentration differences between them suggested that further studies are required to assess the complex aerodynamic movements of the pollutants inside the tunnel. The proposed mobile measurement approach has potential for use in future tunnel studies. Because vehicle exhaust is recognized as one of the main sources of primary and secondary PM in large cities worldwide, there is an increasing need for more frequent and region-specific measurements of EFs in real environments for timely policymaking. Tunnel studies with mobile measurements can provide the required information.\n\n# Author contributions statement', 'summary': 'This study determined the usefulness and advantages of making mobile measurements of exhaust pollutants in a tunnel study.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Mobile measurement of vehicle emission factors in ', 'text': 'Tunnels are the preferred experimental environments for estimating vehicle emission factors (EFs) under real-world driving conditions. In this study, online measurements of traffic-related air pollutants (including  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{O}_{3}$ , particulate matter [PM], and volatile organic compounds [VOCs]) were conducted using a mobile laboratory in the Sujungsan Tunnel in Busan, Korea. Mobile measurements generated concentration profiles of the target exhaust emissions inside the tunnel. These data were used to produce a zonation of the tunnel, i.e., mixing and accumulation zones. There were differences between the  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ , and  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$  profiles, and a starting point that was free from ambient air mixing effects could be set at  $600\\mathrm{m}$  from the tunnel entrance. The EFs of vehicle exhaust emissions were calculated using pollutant concentration gradients. The average EFs for  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ , NO,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{10}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$ , and  $\\sum \\mathrm{VOCs}$  were 149,000, 380, 55, 29.2, 9.64, 4.33, and  $16.7\\mathrm{mgkm}^{-1}\\cdot \\mathrm{veh}^{-1}$ , respectively. Among the VOC groups, alkanes contributed more than  $70\\%$  of the VOC EF. Mobile measurement-derived EFs were validated using the conventional EFs from stationary measurements. The EF results from the mobile measurements matched those from the stationary measurements, while the absolute concentration differences between them implied complex aerodynamic movements of the target pollutants inside the tunnel. This study demonstrated the usefulness and advantages of applying mobile measurements in a tunnel environment and indicated the potential of the approach for observation-based policymaking.\n\n# 1. The safety issues and logistical difficulties in setting up analytical instrumentation inside a tunnel were overcome using a mobile laboratory. The heavy traffic in the urban tunnel did not enable sufficient room for the instrumentation and researchers to operate; thus, safety issues affected the operation of the research. Multipoint data generated by online instruments in a mobile laboratory can also help to overcome the various uncertainties associated with stationary measurements. This study identified a zonation inside the tunnel, i.e., mixing and accumulation zones, and recommended that the mixing zone be avoided to ensure accurate EF measurements. The concept of a concentration gradient was applied for EF calculations. The EF results from the mobile measurements were well matched with those from stationary measurements, while the absolute concentration differences between them suggested that further studies are required to assess the complex aerodynamic movements of the pollutants inside the tunnel. The proposed mobile measurement approach has potential for use in future tunnel studies. Because vehicle exhaust is recognized as one of the main sources of primary and secondary PM in large cities worldwide, there is an increasing need for more frequent and region-specific measurements of EFs in real environments for timely policymaking. The safety issues and logistical difficulties in setting up analytical instrumentation inside a tunnel were overcome using a mobile laboratory. The heavy traffic in the urban tunnel did not enable sufficient room for the instrumentation and researchers to operate; thus, safety issues affected the operation of the research. Multipoint data generated by online instruments in a mobile laboratory can also help to overcome the various uncertainties associated with stationary measurements. This study identified a zonation inside the tunnel, i.e., mixing and accumulation zones, and recommended that the mixing zone be avoided to ensure accurate EF measurements. The concept of a concentration gradient was applied for EF calculations.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Mobile measurement of vehicle emission factors in ', 'text': 'Tunnels are the preferred experimental environments for estimating vehicle emission factors (EFs) under real-world driving conditions. In this study, online measurements of traffic-related air pollutants (including  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{O}_{3}$ , particulate matter [PM], and volatile organic compounds [VOCs]) were conducted using a mobile laboratory in the Sujungsan Tunnel in Busan, Korea. There were differences between the  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ , and  $\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{X}}$  profiles, and a starting point that was free from ambient air mixing effects could be set at  $600\\mathrm{m}$  from the tunnel entrance. The EFs of vehicle exhaust emissions were calculated using pollutant concentration gradients. The average EFs for  $\\mathrm{CO}_{2}$ , NO,  $\\mathrm{NO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{SO}_{2}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{10}$ ,  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$ , and  $\\sum \\mathrm{VOCs}$  were 149,000, 380, 55, 29.2, 9.64, 4.33, and  $16.7\\mathrm{mgkm}^{-1}\\cdot \\mathrm{veh}^{-1}$ , respectively. Among the VOC groups, alkanes contributed more than  $70\\%$  of the VOC EF. Mobile measurement-derived EFs were validated using the conventional EFs from stationary measurements. The EF results from the mobile measurements matched those from the stationary measurements, while the absolute concentration differences between them implied complex aerodynamic movements of the target pollutants inside the tunnel. Introduction\n\nVolatile organic compounds (VOCs) are important precursors that can undergo atmospheric photochemical reactions with nitrogen oxides  $\\left(\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{x}}\\right)$  under ultraviolet radiation to produce secondary products such as ozone  $\\left(\\mathrm{O}_{3}\\right)$  and peroxyacetyl nitrate (PAN) and form photochemical smog (Derwent et al., 2003; Seinfeld and Pandis, 2016). Oxygenated volatile organic compounds (OVOCs) are a class of VOCs with oxygen-containing functional groups, mainly composed of aldehydes, ketones, and alcohols. The concentrations of atmospheric OVOCs vary greatly in different regions. Studies in clean marine areas showed that although phytoplankton in the marine may release OVOCs, such as methanol, acetaldehyde and acetone, their ambient air mixing ratios were usually only a few\n\nto a few hundred pptv (Galbally et al., 2007; Colomb et al., 2009; Wohl et al., 2020), while the concentrations of OVOCs in polluted areas can be as high as dozens of ppbv (Seinfeld and Pandis, 2016; Sheng et al., 2018; Zhou et al., 2019; Maji et al., 2020). The variation in OVOC concentrations is due to the wide variety and complexity of sources of OVOCs. OVOCs can be directly emitted by anthropogenic sources, e.g., solvent volatilization, vehicle emissions (Legreid et al., 2007; Ou et al., 2015), and biogenic sources (Jacob et al., 2002; Mellouki et al., 2015). In addition, OVOCs can also be formed as secondary products by photochemical oxidation of nonmethane hydrocarbons (NMHCs) from anthropogenic and biogenic sources (Yuan et al., 2012; Liu et al., 2015).', 'summary': '© 2020 Elsevier Ltd.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Does energy transition improve air quality_ Eviden', 'text': 'After estimating the negative effects of heating on air quality, we attempted to verify whether the implementation of the WCHP project alleviated air pollution caused by winter heating. This study employed a DID framework by comparing differences in outcomes among pilot cities and non-pilot cities by means of a before-and-after comparison of the clean heating policy. Adopting the procedures of Chen et al. [27], Beck et al. [17], and Moser and Voena [31], we used the following standard DID estimation model in our study:\n\n$$\nY = \\alpha_ {0} + \\gamma W C H P _ {i t} + \\beta X _ {i t} + \\mu_ {i} + \\eta_ {t} + \\varepsilon_ {i t}\n$$\n\nwhere  $WCHP_{it}$  indicates the WCHP policy status of a city. Specifically,  $WCHP_{it} = treated_i \\times period_{it}$ , where  $treated_i$  equals 1 if a given city belongs to pilot cities and 0 otherwise.  $period_{it}$  equals 1 only after a city adopts the WCHP project during the heating period.\n\nWe focused on  $\\gamma$  in this study. The consistent estimation of  $\\gamma$  requires that the WCHP project is a natural experiment; namely, random selection is employed among pilot and non-pilot cities. In order to ensure that the DID model is robust, it is necessary to add some control variables that affect dependent variables. Since the selection is influenced by other key determinants of cities, deviation from the natural experiment will lead to bias of an estimator [18,30,32]. Associated covariates that were endogenous in the selection of pilot cities were identified and included in the regression to control bias. Accordingly, weather conditions, holidays, GDP, the ratio between secondary industries, income levels, and environmental expenditures were included as covariates in our DID model.\n\n# 3.2. The purpose of this study was to determine the contributions of different VOC sources to  $\\mathrm{L_{OH}}$ , OFP, and SOAP using positive matrix factorization (PMF) model. Hourly observation of ambient VOCs at a megacity of Central China was conducted for one month in winter. The  $\\mathrm{L_{OH}}$ , OFP, and SOAP of VOC species were firstly estimated.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Progress of Air Pollution Control in China and Its', 'text': 'The inclusion of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  as a criteria pollutant in the 2012 amendment of NAAQS marked the strategic and philosophical evolvement of air pollution control in China. Ambient  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  concentration had become a more transparent indicator for city residents in China than other air pollutants, as the public began to gradually understand the relationship between  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  pollution, atmospheric visibility, and health impact. The major objectives of the Air Pollution Prevention and Control Action Plan 2013-2017 (Action Plan, hereinafter) launched by the State Council were to improve air quality and reduce heavy pollution days nationwide. Unlike the previous TCZ policy, which was proposed by the SEPA and then approved by the State Council, the formulation of the Action Plan was directly led and promoted by the State Council for the first time in the area of air pollution control. The higher level of authority for the Action Plan reflected the fact that combating  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  pollution would require more coordinated efforts at the national and regional levels than ever before. The European Union defines VOC as any organic compound having an initial boiling point less than or equal to  $250^{\\circ}\\mathrm{C}$  measured at a standard atmospheric pressure of  $101.3\\mathrm{kPa}$  (European Union, 1999).                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Source apportionment of volatile organic compounds', 'text': 'Urban areas in China always suffer from serious haze problems due to high fine particle  $\\mathrm{(PM_{2.5})}$  concentration during wintertime (Zhang and Cao, 2015; Yin et al., 2017; Song et al., 2017). Organic matter (OM) is one of the most important chemical components of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  during winter haze episodes. During the long-lasting haze period in 2013, OM accounted for  $30.5 - 48.0\\%$  of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  masses and secondary organic-rich sources contributed  $12.2 - 25.8\\%$  to  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  at four megacities (Huang et al., 2014). As important precursor gases of secondary organic aerosol (SOA), high concentrations of volatile organic compounds (VOCs) were also observed in haze episodes (Zhang et al., 2014; Wu et al., 2016; Liu et al., 2017; Han et al., 2017). SOA is mainly formed by atmospheric oxidation and condensation of low-volatility VOCs from both anthropogenic and biogenic sources (Hallquist et al., 2016; Chen et al., 2017). Introduction\n\nVolatile organic compounds (VOCs) are important precursors that can undergo atmospheric photochemical reactions with nitrogen oxides  $\\left(\\mathrm{NO}_{\\mathrm{x}}\\right)$  under ultraviolet radiation to produce secondary products such as ozone  $\\left(\\mathrm{O}_{3}\\right)$  and peroxyacetyl nitrate (PAN) and form photochemical smog (Derwent et al., 2003; Seinfeld and Pandis, 2016). Oxygenated volatile organic compounds (OVOCs) are a class of VOCs with oxygen-containing functional groups, mainly composed of aldehydes, ketones, and alcohols. The concentrations of atmospheric OVOCs vary greatly in different regions. Studies in clean marine areas showed that although phytoplankton in the marine may release OVOCs, such as methanol, acetaldehyde and acetone, their ambient air mixing ratios were usually only a few\n\nto a few hundred pptv (Galbally et al., 2007; Colomb et al., 2009; Wohl et al., 2020), while the concentrations of OVOCs in polluted areas can be as high as dozens of ppbv (Seinfeld and Pandis, 2016; Sheng et al., 2018; Zhou et al., 2019; Maji et al., 2020). The variation in OVOC concentrations is due to the wide variety and complexity of sources of OVOCs. OVOCs can be directly emitted by anthropogenic sources, e.g., solvent volatilization, vehicle emissions (Legreid et al., 2007; Ou et al., 2015), and biogenic sources (Jacob et al., 2002; Mellouki et al., 2015). In addition, OVOCs can also be formed as secondary products by photochemical oxidation of nonmethane hydrocarbons (NMHCs) from anthropogenic and biogenic sources (Yuan et al., 2012; Liu et al., 2015).', 'summary': '© 2020 Elsevier Ltd.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Does energy transition improve air quality_ Eviden', 'text': 'After estimating the negative effects of heating on air quality, we attempted to verify whether the implementation of the WCHP project alleviated air pollution caused by winter heating. This study employed a DID framework by comparing differences in outcomes among pilot cities and non-pilot cities by means of a before-and-after comparison of the clean heating policy. Adopting the procedures of Chen et al. [27], Beck et al. [17], and Moser and Voena [31], we used the following standard DID estimation model in our study:\n\n$$\nY = \\alpha_ {0} + \\gamma W C H P _ {i t} + \\beta X _ {i t} + \\mu_ {i} + \\eta_ {t} + \\varepsilon_ {i t}\n$$\n\nwhere  $WCHP_{it}$  indicates the WCHP policy status of a city. Specifically,  $WCHP_{it} = treated_i \\times period_{it}$ , where  $treated_i$  equals 1 if a given city belongs to pilot cities and 0 otherwise.  $period_{it}$  equals 1 only after a city adopts the WCHP project during the heating period.\n\nWe focused on  $\\gamma$  in this study. The consistent estimation of  $\\gamma$  requires that the WCHP project is a natural experiment; namely, random selection is employed among pilot and non-pilot cities. In order to ensure that the DID model is robust, it is necessary to add some control variables that affect dependent variables. Since the selection is influenced by other key determinants of cities, deviation from the natural experiment will lead to bias of an estimator [18,30,32]. Associated covariates that were endogenous in the selection of pilot cities were identified and included in the regression to control bias. Accordingly, weather conditions, holidays, GDP, the ratio between secondary industries, income levels, and environmental expenditures were included as covariates in our DID model.\n\n# 3.2. The purpose of this study was to determine the contributions of different VOC sources to  $\\mathrm{L_{OH}}$ , OFP, and SOAP using positive matrix factorization (PMF) model.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Progress of Air Pollution Control in China and Its', 'text': 'The inclusion of  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  as a criteria pollutant in the 2012 amendment of NAAQS marked the strategic and philosophical evolvement of air pollution control in China. Ambient  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  concentration had become a more transparent indicator for city residents in China than other air pollutants, as the public began to gradually understand the relationship between  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  pollution, atmospheric visibility, and health impact. The major objectives of the Air Pollution Prevention and Control Action Plan 2013-2017 (Action Plan, hereinafter) launched by the State Council were to improve air quality and reduce heavy pollution days nationwide. Unlike the previous TCZ policy, which was proposed by the SEPA and then approved by the State Council, the formulation of the Action Plan was directly led and promoted by the State Council for the first time in the area of air pollution control. The higher level of authority for the Action Plan reflected the fact that combating  $\\mathrm{PM}_{2.5}$  pollution would require more coordinated efforts at the national and regional levels than ever before. This is not easy and makes it difficult to implement new and more chemically detailed mechanisms in models. If done incorrectly, it is similar to errors in emissions speciation or the chemical mechanism used. Nevertheless, making such assignments is often an afterthought in chemical mechanism development and emissions processing, and existing assignments are usually undocumented and have errors and inconsistencies. This work is designed to address some of these problems.\n\n# Introduction\n\nAir quality models need to take differences in how volatile organic compounds (VOCs) react in the atmosphere when predicting effects of their emissions on secondary pollutants such as ozone or secondary organic aerosol. The chemical mechanism is the component of the models that represents how emitted compounds react and form secondary pollutants. Different mechanisms use different model species to represent how organic compounds react, with the number of species in different mechanisms varying by more than an order of magnitude. An important but often overlooked part of the air quality modeling process is determining which model species to use when representing the hundreds of organic compounds that are emitted.\n\nAnthropogenic emissions inventories generally give organic emissions as total mass either of total organic gas (TOG) or of nonexempt (U.S. Code of Federal Regulations, 2014) volatile organic compounds (VOCs) from various sources as a function of time and space, along with codes indicating the emissions sources.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Does energy transition improve air quality_ Eviden', 'text': 'After estimating the negative effects of heating on air quality, we attempted to verify whether the implementation of the WCHP project alleviated air pollution caused by winter heating. This study employed a DID framework by comparing differences in outcomes among pilot cities and non-pilot cities by means of a before-and-after comparison of the clean heating policy. Adopting the procedures of Chen et al. [27], Beck et al. [17], and Moser and Voena [31], we used the following standard DID estimation model in our study:\n\n$$\nY = \\alpha_ {0} + \\gamma W C H P _ {i t} + \\beta X _ {i t} + \\mu_ {i} + \\eta_ {t} + \\varepsilon_ {i t}\n$$\n\nwhere  $WCHP_{it}$  indicates the WCHP policy status of a city. Specifically,  $WCHP_{it} = treated_i \\times period_{it}$ , where  $treated_i$  equals 1 if a given city belongs to pilot cities and 0 otherwise.  $period_{it}$  equals 1 only after a city adopts the WCHP project during the heating period.\n\nWe focused on  $\\gamma$  in this study. The consistent estimation of  $\\gamma$  requires that the WCHP project is a natural experiment; namely, random selection is employed among pilot and non-pilot cities. In order to ensure that the DID model is robust, it is necessary to add some control variables that affect dependent variables. Since the selection is influenced by other key determinants of cities, deviation from the natural experiment will lead to bias of an estimator [18,30,32]. Associated covariates that were endogenous in the selection of pilot cities were identified and included in the regression to control bias. Accordingly, weather conditions, holidays, GDP, the ratio between secondary industries, income levels, and environmental expenditures were included as covariates in our DID model.\n\n# 3.2.                         这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Air quality changes in China 2013-2020_ Effectiven', 'text': 'The increase in population size and economic activity has remarkably increased the demand for fossil fuels in China, posing a severe threat to the environment. However, the recently implemented coal-based energy transition has shifted the energy structure from polluting energies to environment-friendly energies, and the subsequent policies created a great revolution in energy development and environment protection. Nevertheless, the energy distribution and air pollution in China are characterized by regionality, thus, targeting the efficiency of these national control policies, scholars mainly focus on regions with high-polluting and energy-intensive industries, such as Shanxi province and the BJH region; or target a specific policy, such as CTG and CTE policy. Differently, this study revealed the air quality improvement during the implementation of CCTPs at the national level. Clarifying the internal mechanism of these policies is significant when revising and implementing the following policies to achieve sustainable development. The quantitative assessment provided significant results: i) After implementing CCTPs, the Chinese mainland experienced air quality improvement, with the reduction of AQI averaging  $18.82\\%$ ; ii) An identical reduction of air pollution was observed in 2018, indicating a 2-year time lag of the related control policies; iii) There were positive associations between emission reduction promoting, deindustrialization and air quality improvement, suggesting two promising ways to realize sustainable energy development. Through assessing the air quality changes before and after the implementation of CCTPs, it is expected to provide a scientific basis for policymakers and stakeholders to forge consensus on the establishment and enforcement of clean coal policies.\n\n# CRediT authorship contribution statement', 'summary': 'The increase in population size and economic activity has remarkably increased the demand for fossil fuels in China, posing a severe threat to the env...'}, 来自论文ID: air_quality_changes_in_china_2013-2020__effectiven, 关键词: None

                        这个条目的具体内容是: {'title': 'Does energy transition improve air quality_ Eviden', 'text': 'After estimating the negative effects of heating on air quality, we attempted to verify whether the implementation of the WCHP project alleviated air pollution caused by winter heating. This study employed a DID framework by comparing differences in outcomes among pilot cities and non-pilot cities by means of a before-and-after comparison of the clean heating policy. Adopting the procedures of Chen et al. [27], Beck et al. [17], and Moser and Voena [31], we used the following standard DID estimation model in our study:\n\n$$\nY = \\alpha_ {0} + \\gamma W C H P _ {i t} + \\beta X _ {i t} + \\mu_ {i} + \\eta_ {t} + \\varepsilon_ {i t}\n$$\n\nwhere  $WCHP_{it}$  indicates the WCHP policy status of a city. Specifically,  $WCHP_{it} = treated_i \\times period_{it}$ , where  $treated_i$  equals 1 if a given city belongs to pilot cities and 0 otherwise.  $period_{it}$  equals 1 only after a city adopts the WCHP project during the heating period.\n\nWe focused on  $\\gamma$  in this study. The consistent estimation of  $\\gamma$  requires that the WCHP project is a natural experiment; namely, random selection is employed among pilot and non-pilot cities. In order to ensure that the DID model is robust, it is necessary to add some control variables that affect dependent variables. Since the selection is influenced by other key determinants of cities, deviation from the natural experiment will lead to bias of an estimator [18,30,32]. Associated covariates that were endogenous in the selection of pilot cities were identified and included in the regression to control bias. Accordingly, weather conditions, holidays, GDP, the ratio between secondary industries, income levels, and environmental expenditures were included as covariates in our DID model.\n\n# 3.2. Data sources and description', 'summary': 'After estimating the negative effects of heating on air quality, we attempted to verify whether the implementation of the WCHP project alleviated air ...'}, 来自论文ID: does_energy_transition_improve_air_quality__eviden, 关键词: None

## [16:25:53] Hypothesis [Final Report]:: REPORT
**Summary**: ## 科学报告: 中国空气污染控制进展及挑战

### 核心假设
中国在过去几十年中经历了显著的空气污染问题。为应对这一问题，中国政府实施了一系列政策和措施，以减少污染物排放并改善空气质量。本文假设中国的空气污染控制政策在一定程度上达到了预期效果，尤其是在减少PM2.5和其他主要污染物浓度方面，同时面临持续的挑战，如臭氧污染和与气候变化的协同效应。

### 证据链

1. **空气污染控制措施的实施效果**
   - 研究显示，从2014年至2020年，中国通过空气清洁计划实现了PM2.5浓度下降33.65%（ID: 6d8f23ed-637d-4cd1-aad4-f216e7134f72）。
   - 图表展示了2013-2020年间中国AQI的显著下降，平均减少18.82%（ID: 05b1a07c-0922-4fe1-b176-c1993254ab99）。
   - 北京及周边地区的主要前兆物排放在2013-2017年间显著减少，其中SO2减少83%，NOx减少43%，VOCs减少42%，PM2.5减少59%（ID: 1a5185a0-d4db-43dc-ada0-2d4cb54f0e7e）。

2. **空气污染物浓度与健康影响的关联**
   - 研究指出2013年空气污染（包括室内暴露）造成的过早死亡成本接近GDP的10%（ID: 408a9eaa-bd42-434c-8082-c493147700b6）。
   - 研究估算中国在2014-2020年间PM2.5浓度和相关死亡率的变化，表明空气清洁计划对环境和公共卫生产生了巨大效益（ID: a3f186ed-b713-4a25-9377-5c3fe8ebc7b6）。

3. **挑战与未来方向**
   - 除PM2.5外，臭氧和VOCs的控制也变得越来越关键。中国的空气质量管理已从单一污染物控制转向多前体物的综合控制（ID: 83381eea-dac4-4b28-bd31-82bd059715c7）。
   - 气候变化可能削弱亚洲季风，增加O3和PM2.5的浓度。减排指导可能改善空气质量，但也可能增加温室气体排放（ID: 81a3d30e-1df6-46eb-9574-55bc07e9d7ec）。

### 结论

中国在空气污染治理方面取得了显著进展，尤其是减少PM2.5浓度。然而，随着环境治理的深入，臭氧污染的挑战逐渐显现。同时，通过优化能源结构、强化减排措施以及制定综合管理政策，中国可以进一步改善空气质量并应对气候变化带来的多重影响。报告强调持续监测和调整政策，以应对动态的环境变化和新出现的污染问题。
